## 9:21. October MOTM rematch, with Hijo del Villano replacing Villano Jr. (injury) and changed to a lightning match.
4) Templario  (c) DQ Volador Jr. [CMLL MIDDLE]
## 13:13. 4th defense. Templario had Brillante as a second, Volador Jr. had Rugido. Rugido snuck in late in the match to German suplex Templario' Templario kicked out. ## 10:55. Vacant titles (Tessa & Lluvia), final of an eight-team three week tournament. Jarochita & Lluvia become third champions.
3) Titán b Templario [lightning]
## 9:45, via El Inmortal. Salvador Lutteroth Camou (II) was honored after the match, with El Halcon, Mano Negra, Talisman, Tony Salazar, Ringo Mendoza, America Rocca, Satanico and Fantasma joning the younger Salvador Lutteroth for the presentation.
4) Ángel de Oro, Niebla Roja  (c) b Rocky Romero, Volador Jr. [CMLL TAG]
## 21st defense. Originally ended in a DCOR in 19:09 when Volador and Niebla Roja were eliminated and Angel de Oro and Rocky Romero could not make it back in after a Canadian destroyer exchange on the catwalk. Fantasma, Jose Luis Feliciano and Matias Lutteroth came to the ring for the usual post match photo with the champions, but both teams begged for them to allow the match to be restarted. The Chavez made the same request on mic, though Rocky talked about doing the rematch next week. Rocky and Volador finally gave up and started to leave, but the officials were convinced to restart the match. The added fall went 1:27, for a total of 20:36.
5) Máscara Dorada, Místico b Hologram, Komander
## 17:22. Hologram and Dorada went to a double pin, Mistico got Komander with a La Mistica (after Komander tried to do a saluting version of La Mistica to him.) Both teams shook hands post match.
6) Star Jr., Zandokan Jr. b Esfinge, Valiente [relevos suicidas]
## 13:39. Neither team got along, but Star Jr. won it for his team to get to the final.
7) Zandokan Jr. b Star Jr. [mask]
## 15:58. Zandokan won with the Tiger Bomb. Star Jr. is Isaias Lopez Hernadez, 32, 15 years a wrestler. Star Jr. upon masking declared his war with Zandokan was just starting and attacked him.
